#----------------------------------------------------------------
#EDUCATION AND IDEOLOGY
#----------------------------------------------------------------
#//////// Kizuna /////////
#Jukendo Curriculum
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1440801
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1440801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1440801.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JAP
			original_tag = JPC
			original_tag = JPK
			original_tag = JPW
		}
		ROOT = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KIZUNA_COOLDOWN }
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KIZUNA_JUKENDO_ENABLED }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KIZUNA_JUKENDO_REFUSED }
			}
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_educon3tot4
		}
	}
	
	#Enable Jukendo Education
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1440801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1440801.oA"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_educon3tot4 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_educon3tot4jukendo }
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KIZUNA_JUKENDO_ENABLED
	}
	
	#Refuse Jukendo Education
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1440801.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1440801.oB"
		add_political_power = -10
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_KIZUNA_JUKENDO_REFUSED
	}
}

	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1550101.oC"
	}
}

#//////// Special Secrets Protection Act /////////
#Diet's Vote of the Special Secrets Protection Act
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1540901
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Passed
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oA"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.500 }
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength > 0.500 }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_defence_ministry3
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_10 = yes
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1540902 days = 7 } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_PROTECTION_ACT_PASSED
	}
	
	#Steamrolled
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oB"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < 0.500 }
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_defence_ministry3
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_10 = yes
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1540902 days = 7 } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_PROTECTION_ACT_STEAMROLLERED
	}
	
	#Rejected
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oC"
		add_political_power = -200
		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_PROTECTION_ACT_REJECTED
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Passed

			factor = 80
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1541101.oA"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength = 0.667 }
				check_variable = { government_coalition_strength > 0.667 }
			}
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_conspiracy_law
		add_stability = -0.02
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_10 = yes
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1541102 days = 1 } }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_CONSPIRACY_ACT_PASSED
	}
	
	#Steamrollered
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1541101.oB"

			check_variable = { government_coalition_strength < 0.667 }
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_conspiracy_law

		mdmosjap_increase_coalition_party_popularity_10 = yes
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1541102 days = 1 } }

	}
	
	#Rejected

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1540901.oC

		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes

#Operation Amaterasu is a Success!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1541303
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1541303.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1541303.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1541303.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1541303.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_leftwing_government = yes }
			mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_4 = yes
			add_war_support = 0.05
		} else_if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_rightwing_government = yes }
			mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_4 = yes
			add_war_support = 0.05
		} else_if = {
			limit = { trigger_mdmosjap_has_the_islamist_government = yes }
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_4 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_4 = yes
		} else = {
			mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_4 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_4 = yes
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 5.0 name = MDMOSJAP_JAP_operation_amaterasu }
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1541303.oC"
	}
}

#//////// Junior Reserve Officiers' Training Corps /////////
#Form of the Furusato Guards
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1571501
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1571501.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1571501.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JAP
			original_tag = JPC
			original_tag = JPK
			original_tag = JPW
			original_tag = RYU
		}
		ROOT = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_COOLDOWN }
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_propaceducation
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	#Accept the formation of them
	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1571501.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1571501.oA"
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_home_guard_of_japan_TT
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_2 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS
	}
	
	#Force the disbandment of them
	option = {
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1571501.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1571501.oB"
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_2 = yes
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1571511.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1571511.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
#	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JAP
			original_tag = JPC
			original_tag = JPK
			original_tag = JPW
			original_tag = RYU
		}
		OR = {
			JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS }
			JPC = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS }
			JPK = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS }
			JPW = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS }
			RYU = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS }
		}
		ROOT = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_AVAILABLE }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1571511.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1571511.oA"
		custom_effect_tooltip = mdmosjap_unlockdec_home_guards_TT
		hidden_effect = { load_oob = "mdmosjap_JAP_furusato_guards_initial_mobilisation" }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_AVAILABLE
	}
}

#Demobilisation of the Furusato Guards
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1571521
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1571521.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1571521.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
#	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			original_tag = JAP
			original_tag = JPC
			original_tag = JPK
			original_tag = JPW
			original_tag = RYU
		}
		ROOT = {
			NOT = { has_war = yes }
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_AVAILABLE
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_DEBUG_ENABLED }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1571521.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1571521.oA"
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Prefectural Police Squad Guards" disband = yes }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Furusato Guards" disband = yes }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Daigaku Giyuhei" disband = yes }
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_HOKKAIDO }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_HOKKAIDO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_TOHOKU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_TOHOKU
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KANTO }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KANTO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUBU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUBU
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KINKI }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KINKI
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUGOKU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_CHUGOKU
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_SHIKOKU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_SHIKOKU
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KYUSHU }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_KYUSHU
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_OKINAWA }
				clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED_IN_OKINAWA
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_AVAILABLE
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_ASSEMBLED
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_RETIRED }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_JAPAN_JROTC_FURUSATO_GUARDS_RETIRED
		}
	}
}

#Constitutional Contradiction
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1511801
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1511801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1511801.oA"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9contradicted1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_isolation }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_isolation add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_local_security }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_local_security add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = intervention_limited_interventionism }
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = intervention_limited_interventionism add_idea = intervention_regional_interventionism }
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_3 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
	}
}

#//////// Finish Interpretative Amendment of Article 9 /////////	
#Finish of the Interpretative Amendment
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1512101
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1512101.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1512101.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	#Defensive path
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = nationalist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1512101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1512101.oA"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9contradicted2 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9contradicted3L }
		decrease_mdmosjap_concon_left_5 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_3 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_5 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_3 = yes
	}
	
	#Intervention path
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1512101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1512101.oB"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9contradicted2 add_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_holy_article_9contradicted3R }
		decrease_mdmosjap_concon_right_5 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_left_3 = yes
		decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_5 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1631403
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1631403.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1631403.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We support it.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = nationalist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1631403.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1631403.oA"
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ENEMY_CLAUSES_DELETION_SUPPORTING }
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_var = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_did = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_did = mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_max }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1631404 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	#We refuse it.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = nationalist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1631403.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1631403.oB"
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_ENEMY_CLAUSES_DELETION_REFUSING }
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_did = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_did = mdmosjap_un_p5vote_deljapasenemy_max }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1631404 days = 1 } }

			tag = JAP

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1631406.oA"

		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1631406.oB

		}

		NOT = { has_civil_war = yes }
		NOT = { has_border_war = yes }
		OR = {
			has_idea = large_power
			has_idea = great_power
			has_idea = superpower
			has_idea = regional_power
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_P5_CHALLENGE_EXECUTED }

			factor = 100
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1631411.oB

			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1631413.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1631413.oB"
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_JOIN_P5_REFUSING }
		add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_japjoinsp5_did = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { mdmosjap_un_p5vote_japjoinsp5_did = mdmosjap_un_p5vote_japjoinsp5_max }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1631414 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1631414
	hidden = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1631414.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1631414.oD"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_JOIN_P5_REFUSING
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = p5_member }
				country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1631417
			}
		} else = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = p5_member }
				country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1631415
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1631416.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1631416.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1631416.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1631416.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }

		}

	}

#//////// Dragon and Pheasant /////////
#Japan Applies to Join to Our Alliance
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1561701
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1561701.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1561701.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1561701.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1561701.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1561702 }
	}
	
	#We refuse
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { has_government = fascism }
						JAP = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
						JAP = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { has_government = nationalist }
						JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { has_government = democratic }
					JAP = { has_government = democratic }
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { has_government = communism }
					JAP = { has_government = communism }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1561701.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1561701.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1561703 }
	}
}

#China Accepted Our Application!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1561702
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1561702.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1561702.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1561702.oA"
		FROM = { add_to_faction = JAP }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "JAP" value = -400 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "CHI" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "CHI" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "CHI" value = -400 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1561702 days = 1 }
		if = {		#Leave from NATO
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							CHI = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					CHI = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							CHI = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1561712.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1561712.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1561712.oA"
		JAP = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_eastern_great_alliance
			}
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "JAP" value = -400 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "CHI" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "CHI" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "CHI" value = -400 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1561712 days = 1 }
		if = {		#Leave from NATO
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							CHI = { has_idea = NATO_member }

					}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1561721.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1561721.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1561721.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1561721.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_idea = NATO_member } }
			ROOT = {
				remove_ideas = NATO_member
				remove_from_tech_sharing_group = NATO_Tech_Share
			}
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally } }
			ROOT = {
				remove_ideas = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
				remove_from_tech_sharing_group = Major_Non_NATO_Ally_Share
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.1561721
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#ROOT country
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = ROOT
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.oA"
	}
	
	#NATO country
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NATO_member
					has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
				}
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1561721.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member }
					NOT = { has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally }
				}
			}

			modifier = {

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}

			}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1581701.oA"

	}
	
	#We refuse
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {

						JAP = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
						JAP = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { has_government = nationalist }
						JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { has_government = democratic }
					JAP = { has_government = democratic }
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { has_government = communism }
					JAP = { has_government = communism }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1581701.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1581701.oB"

#Russia Accepted Our Application!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1581702
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1581702.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1581702.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1581702.oA"
		FROM = { add_to_faction = JAP }
		JAP = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = CSTO_Tech_Share }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "JAP" value = -400 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "SOV" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "SOV" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "SOV" value = -400 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1581702 days = 1 }
		if = {		#Leave from NATO
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							SOV = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							SOV = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1621712.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1621712.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1621712.oA"
		JAP = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
				create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_JAP_pacific_treaty_association
			}
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "JAP" value = -400 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "USA" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "USA" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "USA" value = -400 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1621712 days = 1 }
		if = {		#Leave from NATO
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							USA = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					USA = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							USA = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
}

#//////// Revive of 1902 /////////
#Japan Applies to Join to Our Alliance
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1641701
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1641701.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1641701.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1641701.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1641701.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1641702 }
	}
	
	#We refuse
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_government = communism }
						JAP = { has_government = communism }
					}
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_government = fascism }
						JAP = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_government = neutrality }
						JAP = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_government = nationalist }
						JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ENG = { has_government = democratic }
					JAP = { has_government = democratic }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1641701.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1641701.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1641703 }
	}
}

#Great Briatin Accepted Our Application!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1641702
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1641702.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1641702.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1641702.oA"
		FROM = { add_to_faction = JAP }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "JAP" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "JAP" value = -400 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "ENG" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "ENG" value = 400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "ENG" value = -400 }
		}
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1641702 days = 1 }
		if = {		#Leave from NATO
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							ENG = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					ENG = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							JAP = { has_idea = NATO_member }
							ENG = { has_idea = NATO_member }
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1561721 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
}

#//////// The Co-Prosperity Strikes Back /////////	
#Japan Founds the Original Alliance - Again
news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1661702.oC"
	}
}

#//////// Final Revision of Article 9 /////////
#End of Japanese Pacifism
news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_nationalism2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	#Japan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oA"
	}
	
	#Asia, Oceania, USA and Russia
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
					NOT = { tag = JAP }
				}
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = australia }
				tag = USA
				tag = SOV
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
					NOT = { tag = SOV }
				}
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = middle_east }
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				AND = {
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = north_america }
					NOT = { tag = USA }
				}
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = south_america }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1611801.oC"
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1732001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1732001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1732001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Yes
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NKO = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
					}
					FROM = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = NKO }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1732001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1732001.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1732002 days = 7 } }
	}
	
	#No
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NKO = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
					}
					FROM = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = NKO }
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1732001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1732001.oB"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1732003 days = 7 } }
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1732002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1732002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1732002.oA"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_JAP_KOR_alliance_by_nf }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_JAP_KOR_alliance_by_nf }
	#	if = {
	#		limit = {
	#			JAP = { is_in_faction = yes }
	#			NKO = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
	#		}
	#		JAP = { add_to_faction = NKO }
	#	}
	#	if = {
	#		limit = {
	#			NKO = { is_in_faction = yes }
	#			JAP = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
	#		}
	#		NKO = { add_to_faction = JAP }
	#	}
	#	if = {
	#		limit = {
	#			JAP = { is_in_faction = yes }
	#			NKO = { is_in_faction = yes }
	#		}
	#		JAP = { leave_faction = yes }
	#		NKO = { add_to_faction = JAP }
	#	}
	#	if = {
	#		limit = {
	#			NKO = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
	#			JAP = { NOT = { is_in_faction = yes } }
	#		}
	#		JAP = {
	#			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_japnko_unification_alliance
	#			add_to_faction = NKO
	#		}
	#	}
		
		ROOT = {
			give_guarantee = FROM
			diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = guarantee active = yes }
		}
		
		NKO = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "JAP" value = 200 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "KOR" value = 1000 }
		}
		KOR = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = force_build_armies value = 100 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "NKO" value = 1000 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "JAP" value = 1000 }
		}
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = protect id = "NKO" value = 200 }
		}
		add_war_support = 0.03
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1732002
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_IMPENDING_JAPANESE_INTERVENTION_IN_KOREAS
	}
}

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1752000
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1752000.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1752000.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = KOR
		JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_MENACE_OF_UNIFICATION }
		KOR = {
			exists = yes
			NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			NOT = { is_subject = yes }
			NOT = { is_puppet = yes }
		}
		NKO = {
			exists = yes
			NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			NOT = { is_subject = yes }
			NOT = { is_puppet = yes }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	
	#Yes
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1752000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752000.oA"
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1752001 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#No
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1752000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752000.oB"
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1752002
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1752002.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1752002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1752002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752002.oA"
		NKO = {
			leave_faction = yes
			add_war_support = 0.10
		}
		KOR = {
			create_faction = mdmosjap_faction_kornko_unification_alliance
			add_to_faction = NKO
			add_war_support = 0.10
		}
		KOR = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = protect id = "NKO" value = 200 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "NKO" value = 200 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "NKO" value = -1000 }
		}
		NKO = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = protect id = "KOR" value = 200 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "KOR" value = 200 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = antagonize id = "KOR" value = -1000 }
		}
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1752002
	}
}

#Retrocession of the Korean Peninsula Occupation Zone
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1732200
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1732200.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1732200.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Return the land to South Korea
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = NKO }
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_force_promise
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_anti_korea_doctrine
				factor = 0.4
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1732200.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1732200.oA"
		if = {		#Dismantle Puppetised North Korean Government
			limit = {
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200308 } }
		}
		if = {		#Give Korean States to South Korea
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 601 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 601 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 601 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 601
				remove_state_claim = 601
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 602 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 602 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 602 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 602
				remove_state_claim = 602
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 603 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 603 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 603 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 603
				remove_state_claim = 603
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 604 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 604 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 604 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 604
				remove_state_claim = 604
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 605 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 605 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 605 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 605
				remove_state_claim = 605
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 606 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 606 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 606 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 606
				remove_state_claim = 606
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 607 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 607 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 607 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 607
				remove_state_claim = 607
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 608 }
				NOT = { KOR = { controls_state = 608 } }
			}
			KOR = { transfer_state = 608 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 608
				remove_state_claim = 608
			}
		}
		every_state = {		#Remove North Korean Claims
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = NKO
				is_owned_by = NKO
			}
			remove_core_of = NKO
			remove_claim_by = NKO
		}
		
		KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1732202 }
	}
	
	#Return the land to North Korea
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_exists = KOR }
				KOR = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1732200.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1732200.oB"
		if = {		#Dismantle Puppetised South Korean Government
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.200308 } }
		}
		if = {		#Give Korean States to North Korea
			limit = {

			}
			NKO = { transfer_state = 601 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 601
				remove_state_claim = 601
			}
		}
		if = {

				ROOT = { controls_state = 602 }
				NOT = { NKO = { controls_state = 602 } }
			}
			NKO = { transfer_state = 602 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 602
				remove_state_claim = 602
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 603 }
				NOT = { NKO = { controls_state = 603 } }
			}
			NKO = { transfer_state = 603 }
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 603
				remove_state_claim = 603

			}

				NOT = { NKO = { controls_state = 606 } }
			}

			NOT = { tag = JAP }

			NOT = { tag = NKO }
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1752201.oB

#Revoke The Refugee Agreement
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1752203
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1752203.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1752203.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1752203.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752203.oA"
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = 0.02
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_KOR_JAP_refugee_agreement_approved }
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = KOR modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_JAP_KOR_alliance_by_nf }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPKOR_REFUGEE_AGREEMENT_REVOKED
		KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1752204 }
		
		JAP = {
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "KOR" value = -400 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "KOR" value = -1000 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = "KOR" value = 1000 }
		}
	}
}

		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_verywell
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752210.oA"
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.200308 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.200308 }
		}
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1752211.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1752211.d

	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1752211.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1752211.oA"
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_ai_strategy = { type = prepare_for_war id = FROM value = 1000 }
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = KOR } }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = NKO value = 3000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = NKO } }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = KOR value = 3000 }
		}
	}

#Form of the Seventh Korean Republic (For Puppetised Korean Country)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1772211
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1772211.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1772211.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1772211.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1772211.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				KOJ = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					remove_state_core = PREV
					remove_state_claim = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				KOJ = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			KOJ = { change_tag_from = NKO }
			KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1772213 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				KOJ = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					remove_state_core = PREV
					remove_state_claim = PREV
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				KOJ = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			KOJ = { change_tag_from = NKO }
			NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1772213 } }
		}
		FROM = { puppet = KOJ }
		if = {
			limit = {
				619 = { is_controlled_by = KOJ }
			}
			KOJ = {
				overlord = { transfer_state = 619 }
				remove_state_core = 619
				remove_state_claim = 619
			}
		}
		KOJ = { hidden_effect = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1772214 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_CHANGE_COUNTRY_TAG_NOTIFICATION_TT
	}
}

#Form of the Seventh Korean Republic (For Japan)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1772212
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1772212.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1772212.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1772212.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1772212.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = NKO }
			}
			KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1772213 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = KOR }
			}
			NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1772213 } }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 601
					state = 602
					state = 603
					state = 604
					state = 605
					state = 606
					state = 607
					state = 608
				}
			}
		#	add_claim_by = KOJ
			add_core_of = KOJ
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { controls_state = 601 }
				NOT = { KOJ = { controls_state = 601 } }
			}
			ROOT = {
				remove_state_core = 601
				remove_state_claim = 601
			}
			KOJ = {
				transfer_state = 601
				add_state_core = 601
			}
			
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.91650102.oA"
		add_political_power = 100
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_5 = yes
			
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_5 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		} else = {
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_3 = yes
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
	}
}

		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620203 hours = 1 } }
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		SOV = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620204 hours = 1 } }
		news_event = { id = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201 days = 1 }

	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JAP
				tag = USA
				tag = KOR
				tag = TAI
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oA"
	}
	
	#CHI, NKO, SOV
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = CHI
				tag = NKO
				tag = SOV
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				NOT = { tag = USA }
				NOT = { tag = KOR }
				NOT = { tag = TAI }
				NOT = { tag = CHI }
				NOT = { tag = NKO }
				NOT = { tag = SOV }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1620201.oC"
	}
}

					is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 3 }

#Historical Domestic Sequence: SDP Leaves Hatoyama's Coalition

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1620207
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1620207.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1620207.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1620207.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1620207.oA"
		add_stability = -0.02
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
		remove_from_array = { gov_coalition_array = 3 }
		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_3_var_1 = yes
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_SDP_LEFT_THE_HATOYAMA_COALITION
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_AGREED
					has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HATOYAMA_LOOPY
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1620210 days = 18 } }	#Hatoyama resigns the cabinet
		}
	}
}

#Henoko Negotiation: Japan's Allotment

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640204
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640204.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640204.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Total Allotment

		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oA
		multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation = 3 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt = 2 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_TOTAL_BEARING
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oA"
	}
	
	#Half Allotment
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oB
		multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation = 2 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt = 1 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_HALF_BEARING
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oB"
	}
	
	#No Allotment

		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oC
		multiply_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation = 1 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt = 0 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_NO_BEARING
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640204.oC"
	}

#Henoko Negotiation: Japan's Plan
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640206
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We Agree This Plan
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation value = 6 compare = less_than }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oA
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1640207 }
		ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = recent_actions_positive } }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oA"
	}
	
	#We Cannot Agree This Plan
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { var = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation value = 6 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oB
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1640208 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640206.oB"
	}
}

#Henoko Negotiation: The United States Agreed
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640207
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640207.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640207.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640207.oA"
		#By the Withdrawal Proposal
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_SMALL_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MEDIUM_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_LARGE_WITHDRAWAL }
			827 = { remove_building = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving } }
			618 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3 }
		}
		
		#By the Allotment Proposal
		if = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt > 0 } }
				add_to_variable = { debt = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt }
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_HenokoNegotiation_TT
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EXTERNAL_DEBT_CHANGE
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt = 0 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_add_debt_HenokoNegotiation_zero_TT
			}
			clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_debt
		}
		
		#By the Replace Location
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_TOHOKU }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			617 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			616 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_CHUBU }
			613 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_SHIKOKU }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			611 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			610 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_TO_IWOJIMA }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			621 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			620 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_MOVE_AND_TRANSFER }
			divide_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving = 2 }
			621 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			620 = { add_building_construction = { type = air_base level = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving instant_build = yes } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640209 days = 1 } }	#Transfer Event
		}
		clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation
		clear_variable = mdmosjap_JAP_var_HenokoNegotiation_moving
		ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_very_positive } }
		add_country_leader_trait = honest
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_HENOKO_NEGOTIATION_AGREED
	}
}

#Claiming the Land in Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660201
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Promise Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_USA_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		827 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1660202 days = 1 } }
		effect_tooltip = { JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_promised } } }
	}
	
	#Reject Japan's Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = CHI
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = TAI
							has_war_with = VIE
							has_war_with = PHI
							has_war_with = MAY
							has_war_with = IND
							has_war_with = RAJ
						}
					}
					any_country = {
						original_tag = NKO
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = KOR
						}
					}
					any_country = {
						original_tag = SOV
						OR = {
							has_war_with = JAP
							has_war_with = USA
							has_war_with = FIN
							has_war_with = SWE
							has_war_with = FRA
							has_war_with = GER
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = UKR
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = TAI
							tag = KOR
						}
						exists = no
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660201.oB"
		add_political_power = -200
		effect_tooltip = { JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_rejected } } }
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1660203 }
	}
}

#U.S. Promises to return the land in Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660202
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_futenma_returning_stage = 0 }
		set_variable = { mdmosjap_var_futenma_returning_stage_tt = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660202.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660202.oA"
		add_political_power = 100
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
			}
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_1 = yes
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_5 = yes
			
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
				}
			}
			increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_5 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_1 = yes
		} else = {
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_left_3 = yes
			decrease_mdmosjap_conrad_right_3 = yes
		}
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		add_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_USA_PROMISED
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_base_removal_promised }
		activate_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj
		hidden_effect = { news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1660202 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1660205
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660205.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660205.oA"
		USA = {
			remove_state_core = 827
		}
		JAP = {
			transfer_state = 827
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1
		}
		if = {	#Support limitedly
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa2 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa2
			add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa_localsupport1 days = 1825 }
		}
		if = {	#Support fully
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3
			add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa_localsupport2 days = 1825 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_RETURN_EVERY_LANDS }
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_RETURN_EVERY_LANDS } }
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_FUTENMA_REDEVELOPMENT }
			827 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_DESTROY_ALL_MILIFACILITIES_TT
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { dockyard > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { air_base > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = air_base level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { radar_station > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = radar_station level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { anti_air_building > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = anti_air_building level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_defense_station > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_defense_station level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { TEL_base > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = TEL_base level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_silo level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { nuclear_reactor > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = nuclear_reactor level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { fuel_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = fuel_silo level = 99 }
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_FUTENMA_JASDF_AIR_BASE }
			827 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_REMAIN_SOME_MILIFACILITIES_TT
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { dockyard > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { missile_silo > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = missile_silo level = 99 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { nuclear_reactor > 0 }
						remove_building = { type = nuclear_reactor level = 99 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		827 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = mdmosjap_temp_var_futenma_new_building_slot
			set_state_name = mdmosjap_rename_STATE_827
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = RYU } }
				hidden_effect = { add_core_of = RYU }
			}
		}
		set_province_name = { id = 7115 name = mdmosjap_rename_VICTORY_POINT_7115 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_USA_HAS_WITHDRAWN
		remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj
		hidden_effect = { news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1660205 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_RECLAIM_FUTENMA_USA_SUSPENDED_WITHDRAW
			remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj
		}
	}
	
	#That bastard!

			factor = 1
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660209.oA

		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = USA }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_broken_promise }
		} else = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_broken_promise_by_war }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa1 }

		}

			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_base_removal_in_okinawa3
		}
		effect_tooltip = { remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj }

	}

			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1660209.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1660209.oB"
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_USA_JAP_broken_promise_by_war_month }
		effect_tooltip = { remove_mission = mdmosjap_JAP_retreat_of_usfj }
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1660211 days = 3 } }
			news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1660209
		}
	}
}

#The Fate of Futenma Base
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1604001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Demand the restitution of Futenma (Add 2 Slots into Okinawa State)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				}
				factor = 0.02
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = JAP_china_encirclement
					CHI = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							is_puppet = no
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oA"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604002 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Ask the United States to maintain there as the U.S.F.J. base
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604001.oB"
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604005 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accpet to Return
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
						has_government = nationalist
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oA"
		FROM = {
			transfer_state = 827
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		ROOT = {
			remove_state_core = 827
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604003 } }
	}
	
	#Refuse to Return
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					CHI = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							is_puppet = no
							is_subject = no
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					RYU = {
						AND = {
							exists = yes
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
								NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = { has_completed_focus = USA_seek_proximity_to_china }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604002.oB"
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1604004 } }
	}
}

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1604011

	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We never forget this (but do nothing)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oA"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
	
	#Now we will take our land by force (Gain the Casus Belli)
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				any_other_country = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = no
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1604011.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1604012.oB"
		add_political_power = -200
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = take_state_focus target = FROM generator = { 827 } }
	}
}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1670401.t

				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1670401.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1670401.oA"
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1670402 days = 7 }
	}
	
	#Establish the Autonomous Prefecture
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1670401.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1670401.oB"

	}
	
	#Neither plans are in my head...
}

#Establishment of Autonomous State of Okinawa
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1670402
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1670402.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1670402.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#New start for Okinawa!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				is_ai = yes
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1670402.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1670402.oA"
		#Core-isation
		RYU = {
			add_state_core = 618
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		#Transferring States
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = RYU
				is_owned_by = JAP
			}
			RYU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		#Puppet-isation
		JAP = {
			puppet = RYU
			set_autonomy = { target = RYU autonomy_state = autonomy_associated_state }
		}
		#Policies by the Suzerain
		RYU = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = RYU_JAP
				REDISTRIBUTE_MDMOSJAP_RYU_GOVERNMENT_SETUP = yes
			}
		}
		
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_10 = yes
	}
	
	#New start for Okinawa! (Play as RYU)
	option = {
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_ai = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1670402.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1670402.oB"
		#Core-isation
		RYU = {
			add_state_core = 618
			add_state_core = 827
		}
		#Transferring States
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = RYU
				is_owned_by = JAP
			}
			RYU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		#Puppet-isation
		JAP = {
			puppet = RYU
			set_autonomy = { target = RYU autonomy_state = autonomy_associated_state }
		}
		#Policies by the Suzerain
		RYU = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = RYU_JAP
				REDISTRIBUTE_MDMOSJAP_RYU_GOVERNMENT_SETUP = yes
			}
		}
		RYU = { change_tag_from = JAP }
		
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_4 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_6 = yes
	}
}

			USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640302 days = 2 } }
			ROOT = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640303 days = 4 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640301.oA"
	}
