#Start Meeting (USA)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640302
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640302.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640302.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 3
	
	#Agree with all of their demands
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
					DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oA"
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_CHALLENGE_TO_SOFA_AGREED_FULLY }
	}
	
	#Reject any of their demands
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
					DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oB"
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_CHALLENGE_TO_SOFA_REJECTED }
	}
	
	#We accuse their own SOFA
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
				DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640302.oC"
		if = {
			limit = { KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640307 days = 3 } }
		} else_if = {
			limit = { DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640310 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

#US Accuses the Japan-Kuwait SOFA
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640307
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640307.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640307.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 3
	
	#Promise the termination of this SOFA
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				factor = 98
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640307.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640307.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_operation_in_IRQ }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_operation_in_IRQ
		}
		KUW = { remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640308 days = 3 } }
	}
	
	#Reject the revision of this SOFA
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640307.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640307.oB"
		add_political_power = -50
		USA = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640309 days = 3 } }
	}
}

					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }

				OR = {
					KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
					DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640308.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640308.oB"

				DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
		#	}
		}

			limit = { DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA } }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640310 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

#Japan Rejects to revise the Japan-Kuwait SOFA
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640309
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640309.t

	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 3
	
	#Forget about it and agree with the revision of our SOFA
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
					DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640309.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640309.oA"
		JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_CHALLENGE_TO_SOFA_AGREED_FULLY }
	}
	
	#Then we just reject the revision of our SOFA
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					KUW = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_KUW_SOFA }
					DJI = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }

	is_triggered_only = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
				}
				factor = 98
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640310.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640310.oA"

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_operation_in_DJI }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_operation_in_DJI
		}
		DJI = { remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_DJI_SOFA }

			}
		}

#//////// Final Agreement of War Crimes /////////
#Proposal to the signing of Final Agreement
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640801
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640801.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Let's propose the \"mutual agreement\" with South Korea.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					AND = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Yukio Hatoyama" }
					}
					#AND = {
					#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					#	has_country_leader = { name = "Japan Regent Congress" }
					#}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640801.oA"
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640802 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#We just apologise for the past war crime.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					AND = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Yukio Hatoyama" }
					}
					#AND = {
					#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					#	has_country_leader = { name = "Japan Regent Congress" }
					#}
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640801.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640801.oB"
		KOR = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640805 days = 1 } }
		add_political_power = -150
	}
}

#Japan Proposes the \"Mutual Final Agreement\" of their past war crime
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640802
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640802.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640802.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept this. For the brighter Korea-Japan friendship.
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640802.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640802.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640803 days = 1 } }
	#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640810 days = 2 }
	#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640811 days = 3 }
		country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640831 days = 550 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KOR_FINAL_AGREEMENT_MUTUAL
	}
	
	#Refuse this. Why should we swallow their forcible agreement again?!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					KOR = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Park Geun-hye" } } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
					JAP = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } }
					JAP = { is_in_faction_with = NKO }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640802.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640802.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640804 days = 1 } }
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640810.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640810.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_FINAL_AGREEMENT_MUTUAL }
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = nationalist }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_20_var_5 = yes
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_21_var_5 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = nationalist } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.10 }
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_5 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_5 = yes
			}
			add_stability = -0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_FINAL_AGREEMENT_TOTAL_APOLOGISE }
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = nationalist }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = nationalist } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.02 }
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_20_var_1 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_21_var_1 = yes

#KOR: Progressivists accuses the government
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640811
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640811.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640811.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640811.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640811.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_FINAL_AGREEMENT_MUTUAL }
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
					}
				}
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_20 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_20 = yes
				add_stability = -0.20
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_1_var_10 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_10 = yes
				add_stability = -0.10
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_2_var_10 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_10 = yes
				add_stability = -0.10
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.30 }
				add_stability = -0.30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAP_FINAL_AGREEMENT_MUTUAL }
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
					}
				}
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_5 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_5 = yes
				add_stability = -0.03
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_1_var_5 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_2_var_5 = yes
				add_stability = -0.02
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
				mdmosjap_decrease_party_popularity_array_2_var_5 = yes
				mdmosjap_increase_party_popularity_array_1_var_5 = yes
				add_stability = -0.02
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
				add_stability = -0.03
			}
			hidden_effect = { recalculate_party = yes update_government_coalition_strength = yes update_party_name = yes set_coalition_drift = yes }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1640831
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1640831.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1640831.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We may abrogate this agreement.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				KOR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Park Geun-hye" } }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640831.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640831.oA"
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1640832 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#There's no any re-considerable thing.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				KOR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Park Geun-hye" } }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					KOR = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Park Geun-hye" } } }
					KOR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Moon Jae-in" } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1640831.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1640831.oB"
		add_political_power = -150
	}
}

#North Korea Accept the Peace Treaty!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1610902
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1610902.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1610902.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1610902.oA"
		if = {
			limit = { NKO = { has_government = democratic } } 
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NKO = { has_government = communism }
					NKO = { has_government = nationalist }
				} 
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NKO = { has_government = fascism } } 
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NKO = { has_government = neutrality }
					NKO = { has_government = nationalist }
				} 
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		mdmosjap_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
			JAP = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_opinion_modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction1 } }
			JAP = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_abduction2 } }
		}
		NKO = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_recognise_south }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_JAP_peace_treaty_approved }
		}
		JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = NKO modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_JAP_peace_treaty_approved } }
		KOR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_recognise_north } }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_abductionleague
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1610904 days = 1 } }
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1610902
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPNKO_PEACE_TREATY_ACCEPTED
	}
}

		}

					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" } }
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
					NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1630804.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1630804.oA"
		NKO = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_japanese_relief2 } }
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1630805
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1630803 days = 365 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Don't need to extend at this moment...
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Koichi Kato" }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}

	#End this joke!

			factor = 10
			modifier = {

					has_country_leader = { name = "Yohei Kono" }

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = mdmosjap_japan.1630810.oA

			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief1 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief1
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_japanese_relief1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief2 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief2
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_japanese_relief2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief3 }
			remove_ideas = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_japanese_relief3
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_japanese_relief3 }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_NKO_japanese_relief_halted }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1730901
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1730901.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1730901.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1730901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1730901.oA"
		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_2 = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		subtract_from_variable = { var = treasury value = 2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_subtract_treasury_senkaku_nationalisation_TT
		939 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_NATIONAL_PROPERTY }
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 2.0 name = MDMOSJAP_JAP_senkaku_nationalisation }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					state = 939
					is_claimed_by = PREV
					NOT = { is_controlled_by = PREV }
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = mdmosjap_opinion_JAP_nationalised_diaoyu }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.91730900 days = 1 }
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1730902 days = 3 } }
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1730901
	}
}

#Mass Violence against Japanese Business, Products and People
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1730903
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1730903.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1730903.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1730903.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1730903.oA"
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.03
		every_owned_state = { damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1.0 } }
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = democratic }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = communism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.03 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.03 }
		}

#Japan Plannning to Dispatch the Naval Fleets for Diaoyu
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1730906
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1730906.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1730906.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#We don't want to make a large conflict
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				827 = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = USA } }
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1730906.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1730906.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1730907 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	#It's a provocation, send our fleets as they wanted
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_CARELESSNESS_ON_SENKAKU }
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				827 = { is_controlled_by = USA }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1730906.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1730906.oB"
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_elections = no } }
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		add_command_power = -20
		navy_experience = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_CARELESSNESS_ON_SENKAKU } }
				country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1730914 days = 2 }
			} else = {
				JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1730908 days = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}

		}

			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }

		}

	#		add_state_core = 939
	#	}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1730917.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1730917.oA"
		add_political_power = 200
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = democratic }
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = communism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.10 }
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_increase_aggression_10_tt
		add_to_variable = { chinese_aggression = 10 }

	}

	title = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Cede to China
	option = {
		trigger = {
			CHI = { exists = yes }
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					has_country_leader_with_trait = pro_china
				}
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					TAI = { has_government = communism }
					ROOT = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					RYU = { exists = yes }
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oA"
		JAP = {
			remove_state_core = 939
			remove_state_claim = 939
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750911 days = 1 }
		}
		939 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }
		#	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_NATIONAL_PROPERTY }
			CHI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		CHI = {
			add_state_core = 939
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1750903
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RYU = { exists = yes } }
			RYU = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750904 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TAI = { exists = yes } }
			TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750906 days = 1 } }
		}
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901
	}
	
	#Cede to Taiwan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			TAI = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			}
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = TAI }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					TAI = { has_government = communism }
					ROOT = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					RYU = { exists = yes }
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oB"
		JAP = {
			remove_state_core = 939
			remove_state_claim = 939
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750911 days = 1 }
		}
		939 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }
		#	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_NATIONAL_PROPERTY }
			TAI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		TAI = {
			add_state_core = 939
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1750903
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RYU = { exists = yes } }
			RYU = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750904 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { exists = yes } }
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750905 days = 1 } }
		}
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901
	}
	
	#Transfer to USA for USFJ
	option = {
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			}
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_reclaim_futenma }
					NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					RYU = { exists = yes }
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oC"
		JAP = {
			remove_state_core = 939
			remove_state_claim = 939
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750911 days = 1 }
		}
		939 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }
		#	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_NATIONAL_PROPERTY }
			USA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		USA = {
			add_state_core = 939
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1750902
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RYU = { exists = yes } }
			RYU = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750904 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { exists = yes } }
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750905 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TAI = { exists = yes } }
			TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750906 days = 1 } }
		}
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901
	}
	
	#Return to RYU
	option = {
		trigger = {
			RYU = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
			}
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = RYU }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 }
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1750901.oD"
		JAP = {
			remove_state_core = 939
			remove_state_claim = 939
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750911 days = 1 }
		}
		939 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_PRIVATE_PROPERTY }
		#	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = DYNAMIC_MODIFIER_MDMOSJAP_JAP_STATE_SENKAKU_NATIONAL_PROPERTY }
			RYU = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		RYU = {
			add_state_core = 939
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1750902
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { exists = yes } }
			CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750905 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TAI = { exists = yes } }
			TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1750905 days = 1 } }
		}
		news_event = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901
	}
}

#Japan Renounces Senkaku Islands
news_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901
	title = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	
	#JAP
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oA"
	}
	
	#CHI, TAI and RYU
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = CHI
				tag = TAI
				tag = RYU
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oB"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				NOT = { tag = CHI }
				NOT = { tag = TAI }
				NOT = { tag = RYU }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1750901.oC"
	}
}

		increase_mdmosjap_concon_right_10 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_left_10 = yes
		increase_mdmosjap_conrad_right_10 = yes
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_political_power = -500
		mdmosjap_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_10 = yes
	}
}

#///////// Offshore Oil Field of Amity /////////
#Acceptance of Taiwan Petroleum Industries in Senkaku 
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770801
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770801.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770801.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept them but our interests matter
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL
		add_political_power = -10
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Give a quarter
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE
		add_political_power = -20
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Fifty-fifty is the way to promise
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770801.oC"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE
		add_political_power = -40
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Japan's offer of the oil interests in Diaoyutai
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770802
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = { 
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 2 }
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 4 }
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					add_resource = { type = oil amount = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Accept their offer
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770803 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Refuse and keep our claim
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL }
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE }
				add = 25
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770802.oB"
		FROM = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770805 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Taiwan accepted our offer
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770803
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770803.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770803.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770803.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770803.oA"
		if = { 
			limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL } }
			add_political_power = 20
			939 = { add_resource = { type = oil amount = -2 } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE } }
			add_political_power = 40
			939 = { add_resource = { type = oil amount = -4 } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
			add_political_power = 80
			939 = { add_resource = { type = oil amount = -8 } }
		}
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1770804 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#The oil interests agreement goes into effect
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1770804
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1770804.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1770804.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1770804.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1770804.oA"
		if = { 
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_SMALL } }
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_capital = yes }
				add_resource = { type = oil amount = 2 }
			}
			add_political_power = 20
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_MIDDLE } }
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_capital = yes }
				add_resource = { type = oil amount = 4 }
			}
			add_political_power = 40
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_AMITY_OIL_FIELD_TAI_INTERESTS_LARGE } }
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_capital = yes }
				add_resource = { type = oil amount = 8 }
			}
			add_political_power = 80
		}
		939 = {
			remove_core_of = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}

#//////// Terminus of the Belt and Road /////////
#Japan Proposes to Join to the SCO
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1731001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1731001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1731001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Agree
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = JAP value < -59 } }	#49+10
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = JAP value < -84 } }	#74+10
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = JAP value < -109 } }	#99+10
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1731001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1731001.oA"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1731002 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Disagree
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = JAP value < -59 } }	#49+10
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {

#The Detail of Apology - To Which Country?
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1751001
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1751001.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1751001.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Apologise to Continental China
	option = {
		trigger = {
			CHI = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_china_encirclement }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				TAI = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.01
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = pro_china
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oA"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_CHI
		#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751004 days = 3 }
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751005 days = 4 } }
	#	custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_ONGOING_TT
	}
	
	#Apologise to Taiwan
	option = {
		trigger = {
			TAI = { exists = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.01
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oB"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_TAI
		#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751004 days = 3 }
		}
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751006 days = 4 } }
	#	custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_ONGOING_TT
	}
	
	#Apologise to Both
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				CHI = { exists = yes }
				TAI = { exists = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					has_government = nationalist
				}
				factor = 0.9
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1751001.oC"
		JAP = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_BOTH
		#	country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751004 days = 3 }
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751005 days = 4 } }
		TAI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1751006 days = 7 } }	#Time lag for sequel events
	#	custom_effect_tooltip = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_NANJING_ONGOING_TT
	}
}

#Japan Send Message of Apology for Nanjing (CHI)
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1751005
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1751005.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1751005.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept Their Apology
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.99
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
					#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
					#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					#	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_ARTICLE_9
						has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ADAPT_STATE_EMERGENCY_PREROGATIVE
						has_completed_focus = JAP_china_encirclement
						has_government = nationalist
						is_justifying_wargoal_against = CHI
						has_wargoal_against = CHI
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1751005.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1751005.oA"
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_war_support = -0.02
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1751007 }
	}
	
	#Refuse Their Apology
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_NATIONALISE_SENKAKU }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_USA_DEFENDS_SENKAKU }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = CHI
						is_puppet_of = CHI
						is_subject_of = CHI
						NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1751005.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1751005.oA"
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = 0.02
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1751008 }
	}
}

	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1582302.d

	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_ANTICCP_G7_SANCTION_PROPOSAL_RECEIVED
		}
	}
	
	#Take part in
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Donald Trump" } }
				factor = 2.5
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = TAI
						has_war_with = TIB
						has_war_with = HKG
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_Consider_Electoral_Reform_in_Hong_Kong
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_Pressure_the_SARs
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				CHI = {
					NOT = { controls_state = 592 }	#Xinjiang
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				HKG = {
					NOT = { is_puppet_of = CHI }
					NOT = { is_subject_of = CHI }
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_government = communism }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = sco_member
						has_idea = sco_observer
						has_idea = sco_member_econ
						has_idea = sco_member_pol
						has_idea = sco_member_mil
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1582302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1582302.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1582303 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_ANTICCP_G7_SANCTION_PROPOSAL_AGREED
	}
	
	#Shrug off
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Putin" } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Donald Trump" } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_government = democratic }
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1582302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1582302.oA"
		FROM = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1582304 }
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_ANTICCP_G7_SANCTION_PROPOSAL_REFUSED
	}

	id = mdmosjap_japan.1582303
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1582303.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1582303.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_g7sanction_member_count = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.generic_great
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1582303.oA"
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_idea = g7_member
					NOT = { tag = CHI }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_ANTICCP_G7_SANCTION_PROPOSAL_RECEIVED }
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = g7_member
					NOT = { tag = JAP }
					NOT = { tag = JPC }
					NOT = { tag = JPK }
					NOT = { tag = JPW }
					NOT = { tag = CHI }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_ANTICCP_G7_SANCTION_PROPOSAL_RECEIVED }
				}
				country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1582302 days = 1 }
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { mdmosjap_JAP_var_anticcp_g7sanction_member_count = 0 } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1582308 days = 1 }
		} else = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1582305 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

#Japan Requests the South Korean Support
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682302
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Agree the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
					JAP = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = NATO_member
							has_idea = Major_Non_NATO_Ally
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_anti_korea_doctrine }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_government = nationalist }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_KOR_SUPPORT_ACCEPTED
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682303 days = 2 } }
	}
	
	#Refuse the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				JAP = { has_completed_focus = JAP_new_allied_member }
				factor = 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				NKO = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { exists = yes }
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NKO = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682302.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_KOR_SUPPORT_REFUSED
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682310 days = 2 } }
	}
}

		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682304 hours = 1 } }

			limit = { NKO = { exists = yes } }
			NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682305 }

#Japan Requests an Alternative Guarantee to North Korea
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682313
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682313.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682313.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Agree the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_POOR_PYONGYANG_STATEMENT } }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oA"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_ACCEPTED
		add_stability = -0.02
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682314 days = 2 } }
	}
	
	#Refuse the request
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPNKO_PEACE_TREATY_ACCEPTED }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_ai = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oB"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_REFUSED
		add_stability = 0.03
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682316 days = 2 } }
	}
	
	#Demand to Lift All Sanction then Set Up Reparative Aids, Instead of Forsake China
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682313.oC"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682341 days = 2 } }
	}
}

#North Korea Accepts the Japan's Guarantee Instead of the China's
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682314
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682314.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682314.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682314.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682314.oA"
		ROOT = {
			give_guarantee = NKO
			diplomatic_relation = { country = NKO relation = guarantee active = yes }
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682315 hours = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { KOR = { exists = yes } }
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682321 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1 } }
			JAP = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_NKOcompensation_1 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_2 } }
			JAP = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_NKOcompensation_2 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_3 } }
			JAP = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_anticcp_NKOcompensation_3 days = 1825 } }
		}
	#	if = {
	#		limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_TOTALCONCESSION } }
	#	}
		set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_IMPENDING_JAPANESE_INTERVENTION_IN_KOREAS
	}
}

#North Korea Threw the China's Security Over
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682315
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682315.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682315.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682315.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682315.oA"
		ROOT = {
			diplomatic_relation = { country = NKO relation = guarantee active = no }
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.03
	}
}

#North Korea Rejects the Alternative Guarantee
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682316
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	option = {
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682316.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682316.oA"
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {			# RoK didn't reject yet, propose to RoK
			limit = {
				KOR = { exists = yes }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_KOREAN_INTERVENTION_SOUTH_KOREA_REFUSED_GUARANTEE }
			}
			KOR = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682322 }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_JAP_KOREAN_INTERVENTION_NORTH_KOREA_REFUSED_GUARANTEE
		} else = {		# RoK already rejected, end event cycle
			set_global_flag = MDMOSJAP_EVENT_IMPENDING_JAPANESE_INTERVENTION_IN_KOREAS
		}
	}
}

#Japan Guarantees North Korea!
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682321
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682321.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682321.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	#Protest
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
			modifier = {
				any_other_country = {
					NOT = { tag = JAP }
					NOT = { tag = JPC }
					NOT = { tag = JPK }
					NOT = { tag = JPW }
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
					is_major = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				USA = {
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oA"
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = loyal_to_our_enemy }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682323 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Tolerate
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				any_other_country = {
					NOT = { tag = JAP }
					NOT = { tag = JPC }
					NOT = { tag = JPK }
					NOT = { tag = JPW }
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
					is_major = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				USA = {
					has_guaranteed = ROOT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oB"
		add_stability = -0.10
	}
	
	#Refuse Japanese Guarantee
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682321.oC"
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = loyal_to_our_enemy }
		JAP = {
			hidden_effect = { diplomatic_relation = { country = KOR relation = guarantee active = no } }
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682324 }
		}
	}
}

#North Korea Demands to Lift All Sanction then Set Up Reparative Aids, Instead of Forsaking China
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682341
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682341.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682341.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept the Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oA"
		add_political_power = -20
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682342 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Revoke the Negotiation
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oB"
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682349 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#Counter-Conditioning: Accept Entering Japanese Investigators to Search Abductees
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_idea = idea_mdmosjap_JAP_abductionleague
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oC"
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682351 days = 2 } }
	}
}

#Japan Accepts Our Demand
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682342
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Let's Sign the Agreement!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oA"
		add_stability = 0.03
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_ACCEPTED
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES } }
			set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_ALLOWED_TO_SEARCH_FOR_ABDUCTEES
		}
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1682314 }
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_1 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_2 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_2 days = 1825 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { JAP = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_3 } }
			NKO = { add_timed_idea = { idea = idea_mdmosjap_NKO_anticcp_NKOcompensation_3 days = 1825 } }
		}
	}
	
	#Demand More! They Should Accept Building the Nuclear Power Plant!
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_JAPNKO_PEACE_TREATY_ACCEPTED }
				factor = 0.04
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-il" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-Un" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-un" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-chul" } }
						NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Yo-jong" } }
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682342.oB"
		JAP = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682343 days = 2 } }
	}
}

#North Korea Adds the Demand to Accept Building the Nuclear Power Plant
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_japan.1682343
	title = mdmosjap_japan.1682343.t
	desc = mdmosjap_japan.1682343.d
	#picture = GFX_news_event_hearts_of_iron_4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Accept the Demand
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = nationalist
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682343.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682343.oA"
		add_political_power = -40
		clr_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_1
		set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_NF_ANTICCP_NKO_SUPPORT_NEGOTIATION_2
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682344 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	#That Would Be Not Accepted
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682343.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682341.oB"
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682349 days = 2 } }
	}
	
	#Revoke the Negotiation
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japan.1682343.oC
		add_political_power = -60
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japan.1682343.oC"
		NKO = { country_event = { id = mdmosjap_japan.1682350 days = 1 } }
	}
}

		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oB"
	}
	
	#TAI
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = TAI
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oC"
	}
	
	#The others
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				NOT = { tag = TAI }
				NOT = { tag = CHI }
			}
		}
		name = mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mdmosjap_japannews.1642301.oD"
	}
}
